\subsection{Description détaillée}
This file contains all the types and functions that define the interface between a D\-R\-I driver and driver loader. Currently, the most common driver loader is the X\-Free86 lib\-G\-L.\-so. However, other loaders do exist, and in the future the server-\/side libglx.\-a will also be a loader.

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Auteur}
Kevin E. Martin \href{mailto:kevin@precisioninsight.com}{\tt kevin@precisioninsight.\-com} 

Ian Romanick \href{mailto:idr@us.ibm.com}{\tt idr@us.\-ibm.\-com} 

Kristian Høgsberg \href{mailto:krh@redhat.com}{\tt krh@redhat.\-com} 
\end{DoxyAuthor}


Définition dans le fichier \hyperlink{dri__interface_8h_source}{dri\-\_\-interface.\-h}.

For example, on little endian \-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-I\-M\-A\-G\-E\-\_\-\-F\-O\-R\-M\-A\-T\-\_\-\-X\-R\-G\-B8888 corresponds to M\-E\-S\-A\-\_\-\-F\-O\-R\-M\-A\-T\-\_\-\-X\-R\-G\-B8888, but M\-E\-S\-A\-\_\-\-F\-O\-R\-M\-A\-T\-\_\-\-X\-R\-G\-B8888\-\_\-\-R\-E\-V on big endian. 

Définition à la ligne 905 du fichier dri\-\_\-interface.\-h.

Définition à la ligne 906 du fichier dri\-\_\-interface.\-h.

\hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_a0196a75d9fea890a1100becea08626d0}{\index{dri\-\_\-interface.\-h@{dri\-\_\-interface.\-h}!\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-I\-M\-A\-G\-E\-\_\-\-L\-O\-O\-K\-U\-P@{\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-I\-M\-A\-G\-E\-\_\-\-L\-O\-O\-K\-U\-P}}

\subsubsection[{\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-I\-M\-A\-G\-E\-\_\-\-L\-O\-O\-K\-U\-P}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define \-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-I\-M\-A\-G\-E\-\_\-\-L\-O\-O\-K\-U\-P~\char`\"{}D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-I\-M\-A\-G\-E\-\_\-\-L\-O\-O\-K\-U\-P\char`\"{}}}\label{dri__interface_8h_a0196a75d9fea890a1100becea08626d0}
This extension must be implemented by the loader and passed to the driver at screen creation time. The E\-G\-L\-Image entry points in the various client A\-P\-Is take opaque E\-G\-L\-Image handles and use this extension to map them to a \-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-Iimage. At version 1, this extensions allows mapping E\-G\-L\-Image pointers to \-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-Iimage pointers, but future versions could support other E\-G\-L\-Image-\/like, opaque types with new lookup functions.

\index{\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-U\-S\-E\-\_\-\-I\-N\-V\-A\-L\-I\-D\-A\-T\-E@{\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-U\-S\-E\-\_\-\-I\-N\-V\-A\-L\-I\-D\-A\-T\-E}!dri_interface.h@{dri\-\_\-interface.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-U\-S\-E\-\_\-\-I\-N\-V\-A\-L\-I\-D\-A\-T\-E}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define \-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-U\-S\-E\-\_\-\-I\-N\-V\-A\-L\-I\-D\-A\-T\-E~\char`\"{}D\-R\-I\-\_\-\-Use\-Invalidate\char`\"{}}}\label{dri__interface_8h_aaee2bd066961d913a534a8fa5b6a2763}
Invalidate loader extension. The presence of this extension indicates to the D\-R\-I driver that the loader will call invalidate in the \-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-I2\-\_\-\-F\-L\-U\-S\-H extension, whenever the needs to query for new buffers. This means that the D\-R\-I driver can drop the polling in \hyperlink{gl_8h_a8e93835e91933b7078c88f905dd8599c}{gl\-Viewport()}.

The extension doesn't provide any functionality, it's only use to indicate to the driver that it can use the new semantics. A D\-R\-I driver can use this to switch between the different semantics or just refuse to initialize if this extension isn't present. 

Définition à la ligne 455 du fichier dri\-\_\-interface.\-h.

\hypertarget{dri__interface_8h_a30777449fbcbb41d376496533cfe7907}{\index{dri\-\_\-interface.\-h@{dri\-\_\-interface.\-h}!\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-Iget\-Drawable\-Info\-Extension@{\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-Iget\-Drawable\-Info\-Extension}}
\index{\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-Iget\-Drawable\-Info\-Extension@{\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-Iget\-Drawable\-Info\-Extension}!dri_interface.h@{dri\-\_\-interface.\-h}}
\subsubsection[{\-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-Iget\-Drawable\-Info\-Extension}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef struct {\bf \-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-Iget\-Drawable\-Info\-Extension\-Rec} {\bf \-\_\-\-\_\-\-D\-R\-Iget\-Drawable\-Info\-Extension}}}\label{dri__interface_8h_a30777449fbcbb41d376496533cfe7907}
The following extensions describe loader features that the D\-R\-I driver can make use of. Some of these are mandatory, such as the get\-Drawable\-Info extension for D\-R\-I and the D\-R\-I Loader extensions for D\-R\-I2, while others are optional, and if present allow the driver to expose certain features. The loader pass in a N\-U\-L\-L terminated array of these extensions to the driver in the create\-New\-Screen constructor.
